Tips:
- Generic or literal annotations might be in use. If so, try using: --eval-annotations
  But check the caveat section: https://github.com/netromdk/vermin#caveats
- You're using potentially backported modules: argparse, asyncio, configparser, dataclasses, enum, faulthandler, importlib, typing, typing_extensions
  If so, try using the following for better results: --backport argparse --backport asyncio --backport configparser --backport dataclasses --backport enum --backport faulthandler --backport importlib --backport typing --backport typing_extensions
- Since '# novm' or '# novermin' weren't used, a speedup can be achieved using: --no-parse-comments
